## Basil Complete Novel By Huma Waqas

## Rude Hero Based Urdu Novel

Basil aka Duran who is Hero in this novel is quite Rude and hard to understand personality who has been living a tough life since childhood. That makes him so rude and extraordinary person. He did a lot in his childhood that was ultimately making him tough and when the story goes on you can see big changes coming in the story with tragic turns. Read Basil By Huma Waqas.

Huma Waqas completed her Bachelor's degree in English Literature from the University of Karachi. She went on to pursue a Master's degree in the same field from the same university.
